24 /**
25  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
26  */
27 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
28                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
29                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
30                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
31                                 val userService: UserService)
32     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
33     extends AbstractController(cc)
34     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
35     with Util {
36 
37   val log = Logger("api.event")
38 
39   def getEvent(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
40     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
41 
42     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
43 
44     db.run(q.detailed).map(x => x.headOption match {
45       case Some(r) => Ok(Json.toJson(r))
46       case _ => NotFound
47     })
48   }
49 
50   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Int], category: Option[Int],
51                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
52     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
53 
54     val q = for {
55       e <- event if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""
56                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
57                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1).bind === 0 || location.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
58                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
59     } yield e
60 
61     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
62     returnPaged(s,q,db)
63   }
64 
65   def getNearby(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
66     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
67 
68     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
69 
70     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
71       case Some(e) => {
72         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
73           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude, e.location.longitude, y._2.latitude, y._2.longitude))
74           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
75         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
76         returnPaged(s,q,db)
77       }
78       case None => Future(NotFound)
79     }
80   }
81 
82   def getSameViewed(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
83     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
84 
85     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
86       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
87       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
88       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
89 
90     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
91 
92     returnPaged(s,q,db)
93   }
94 
95   def deleteEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
96     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
97 
98     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
99 
100     db.run(q).map {
101       case 0 => NotFound
102       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
103     }
104   }
105 
106   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
107     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
108       form => {
109         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
110       },
111       data => {
112         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
113 
114         val locationQuery = (data.location.id match {
115           case None => insertAndReturn[Location,LocationTable](LocationTable.location,data.location)
116           case Some(id) => LocationTable.location.filter(_.id === id).result.map(_.head)
117         })
118 
119         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
120 
121         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
122           data.categories.map {
123             case cat =>
124               cat.id match {
125                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
126                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
127               }
128           }).map(_.flatten)
129 
130         db.run(locationQuery.zip(imagesQuery).zip(categoriesQuery)).flatMap { case ((location,images),categories) =>
131           val event = Event(None, data.name, data.from, data.to, data.description, organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1))
132           db.run(insertAndReturn[Event,EventTable](EventTable.event,event)).map(r => (r,images,categories))
133         }.flatMap { case (event,images,categories) =>
134           val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event,img._2))
135           val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
136           val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
137           db.run(imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed)
138         }.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x.head)))
139       })
140   }
141 
142   def updateEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
143     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
144       form => {
145         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
146       },
147       data => {
148         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
149 
150         val locationQuery = (data.location.id match {
151           case None => insertAndReturn[Location,LocationTable](LocationTable.location,data.location)
152           case Some(id) => LocationTable.location.filter(_.id === id).result.map(_.head)
153         })
154 
155         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
156 
157         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
158           data.categories.map {
159             case cat =>
160               cat.id match {
161                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
162                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
163               }
164           }).map(_.flatten)
165 
166         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
167 
168         db.run(locationQuery.zip(imagesQuery).zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).flatMap {
169           case (((location,images),categories),Some(event)) => {
170             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to, data.description, organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1))
171 
172             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
173 
174             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
175               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
176           }
177           case (((_,_),_),None) => Future.successful(None)
178         }.flatMap {
179           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
180             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
181             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
182             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
183 
184             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event, img._2))
185             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
186             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
187             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
188           }
189           case None => Future.successful(None)
190         }.map {
191           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
192           case None => BadRequest
193         }
194       })
195   }
196 
197   def participate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
198     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
199 
200     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
201       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).result)
202 
203     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
204       case (Some(e),None) => {
205         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1),id)))
206         Future.successful(Ok)
207       }
208       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
209       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
210     }
211   }
212 
213   def unparticipate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
214     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
215 
216     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).delete)
217       .flatMap {
218       case 1 => {
219         Future.successful(Ok)
220       }
221       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
222     }
223   }
